regular expression 정규식¶

In [1]:
import re
In [2]:
content = "Hello World"
dot = re.compile("(H..).(o..)")
plus = re.compile("l+")
In [3]:
re.search(dot, content)
Out[3]:
<_sre.SRE_Match object; span=(0, 7), match='Hello W'>
In [4]:
re.search(plus, content)
Out[4]:
<_sre.SRE_Match object; span=(2, 4), match='ll'>
In [5]:
print(re.findall(plus, content))

['ll', 'l']
In [6]:
data = """
park = 800905-1049118
kim 700905-1059119
"""

pattern = re.compile("(\d{6})[-](\d{7})")

print(pattern, data)
print(re.findall(pattern, data))
print(pattern.sub("\g<1>-*******", data))

re.compile('(\\d{6})[-](\\d{7})') 
park = 800905-1049118
kim 700905-1059119

[('800905', '1049118'), ('700905', '1059119')]

park = 800905-*******
kim 700905-*******

print(m)

In [23]:

In [26]:
p = re.compile(r"(\w+) (\w+)")
result = re.search(p, "Issac Newton, physicist")
print(result.group())
print(result.group(1), result.group(2), result.group(1,2))

Issac Newton
Issac Newton ('Issac', 'Newton')
In [28]:
p.sub("\g<2> \g<1>", "Isaac Newton, physicist")
Out[28]:
'Newton Isaac, physicist'
In [29]:
data = """
acccb
a....b
aaab
a.cccb
"""
p = re.compile("a[.]{3,}b")

p = re.compile("[.]")
In [30]:

Out[30]:
'.'
In [31]:
data = """
park 010-9999-9988
kim 010-9909-7789
lee 010-8789-7768
"""
p = re.compile(r"(\w+)(\s+)(\d+)[-](\d+)[-](\d+)")
result = p.findall(data)
print(p.sub("\g<1> \g<3>-\g<4>-####",data))

park 010-9999-####
kim 010-9909-####
lee 010-8789-####
In [32]:
data = """
park@naver.com
kim@daum.net
lee@myhome.co.kr
"""

p = re.compile(".*[@].*[.][^(com)|(net)]")
p.findall(data)
Out[32]:
['lee@myhome.co.k']
